{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_php_office_1_1_php_spreadsheet_1_1_reader_1_1_xls_ae39f1c3e959dc3d475d342492116f917} 
Php\+Office\textbackslash{}\+Php\+Spreadsheet\textbackslash{}\+Reader\textbackslash{}\+Xls\+::get\+Spliced\+Record\+Data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}

Reads a record from current position in data stream and continues reading data as long as CONTINUE records are found. Splices the record data pieces and returns the combined string as if record data is in one piece. Moves to next current position in data stream to start of next record different from a CONt\+INUE record.

DATEMODE.

This record specifies the base date for displaying date values. All dates are stored as count of days past this base date. In BIFF2-\/\+BIFF4 this record is part of the Calculation Settings Block. In BIFF5-\/\+BIFF8 it is stored in the Workbook Globals Substream.

DEFINEDNAME.

This record is part of a Link Table. It contains the name and the token array of an internal defined name. Token arrays of defined names contain tokens with aberrant token classes.

FILEPASS.

This record is part of the File Protection Block. It contains information about the read/write password of the file. All record contents following this record will be encrypted.

-- "{}\+Open\+Office.\+org\textquotesingle{}s Documentation of the Microsoft         Excel File Format"{}

The decryption functions and objects used from here on in are based on the source of Spreadsheet-\/\+Parse\+Excel\+: \href{https://metacpan.org/release/Spreadsheet-ParseExcel}{\texttt{ https\+://metacpan.\+org/release/\+Spreadsheet-\/\+Parse\+Excel}} \Hypertarget{class_php_office_1_1_php_spreadsheet_1_1_reader_1_1_xls_a6f00b62e43137c9d3a94e6605ee21b7b}\index{PhpOffice\textbackslash{}PhpSpreadsheet\textbackslash{}Reader\textbackslash{}Xls@{PhpOffice\textbackslash{}PhpSpreadsheet\textbackslash{}Reader\textbackslash{}Xls}!readFont@{readFont}}

FORMAT.

This record contains information about a number format. All FORMAT records occur together in a sequential list.

In BIFF2-\/\+BIFF4 other records referencing a FORMAT record contain a zero-\/based index into this list. From BIFF5 on the FORMAT record contains the index itself that will be used by other records.

-- "{}\+Open\+Office.\+org\textquotesingle{}s Documentation of the Microsoft         Excel File Format"{} \Hypertarget{class_php_office_1_1_php_spreadsheet_1_1_reader_1_1_xls_abcd5a3d8e50a57bc7f24738286d9ea0e}\index{PhpOffice\textbackslash{}PhpSpreadsheet\textbackslash{}Reader\textbackslash{}Xls@{PhpOffice\textbackslash{}PhpSpreadsheet\textbackslash{}Reader\textbackslash{}Xls}!readFormula@{readFormula}}

Read RK record This record represents a cell that contains an RK value (encoded integer or floating-\/point value). If a floating-\/point value cannot be encoded to an RK value, a NUMBER record will be written. This record replaces the record INTEGER written in BIFF2.

ROW.

This record contains the properties of a single row in a sheet. Rows and cells in a sheet are divided into blocks of 32 rows.

Read a SHAREDFMLA record. This function just stores the binary shared formula in the reader, which usually contains relative references. SHEET.

This record is located in the Workbook Globals Substream and represents a sheet inside the workbook. One SHEET record is written for each sheet. It stores the sheet name and a stream offset to the BOF record of the respective Sheet Substream within the Workbook Stream.

SST -\/ Shared String Table.

This record contains a list of all strings used anywhere in the workbook. Each string occurs only once. The workbook uses indexes into the list to reference the strings.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_php_office_1_1_php_spreadsheet_1_1_reader_1_1_xls_a8ee39ca70f04d7234dca94f09e3ca15d} 
Php\+Office\textbackslash{}\+Php\+Spreadsheet\textbackslash{}\+Reader\textbackslash{}\+Xls\+::read\+Xf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}

XF -\/ Extended Format.

This record contains formatting information for cells, rows, columns or styles. According to \href{https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/147732}{\texttt{ https\+://support.\+microsoft.\+com/en-\/us/help/147732}} there are always at least 15 cell style XF and 1 cell XF. Inspection of Excel files generated by MS Office Excel shows that XF records 0-\/14 are cell style XF and XF record 15 is a cell XF We only read the first cell style XF and skip the remaining cell style XF records We read all cell XF records.

-- "{}\+Open\+Office.\+org\textquotesingle{}s Documentation of the Microsoft         Excel File Format"{} \Hypertarget{class_php_office_1_1_php_spreadsheet_1_1_reader_1_1_xls_a1e62e68135eeb1d17bde37483de53177}\index{PhpOffice\textbackslash{}PhpSpreadsheet\textbackslash{}Reader\textbackslash{}Xls@{PhpOffice\textbackslash{}PhpSpreadsheet\textbackslash{}Reader\textbackslash{}Xls}!readXfExt@{readXfExt}}
